 from (SELECT       a.F10003 AS Marca, u1.F70104 AS EID, dbo.F062.F06205 AS CentruCost, a.F10008 + '  ' + a.F10009 AS Nume, a.F100894 AS Mail, SUBSTRING(g.F00608, 0, 20) AS Departament, 
                         g.F00607 AS cod_Departament, f.F00506 AS cod_Divizie, dbo.F004.F00405 AS cod_filiala, a.F10022 AS DataAngajarii, a.F10023 AS DataPlecarii, ISNULL(b.Cuvenite, 0) AS cuvenite, ISNULL(b.Efectuate, 0) 
                         AS efectuateanterior, ISNULL(b.SoldAnterior, 0) AS soldanterior, ISNULL(b.SoldAnterior, 0) + ISNULL(b.Cuvenite, 0) AS TotalCuvenite, SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua) = 1 AND ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) 
                         AS CO_01, SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua) = 2 AND ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_02, SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua) = 3 AND ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_03, 
                         SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua) = 4 AND ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_04, SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua) = 5 AND ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_05, SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua)
                          = 6 AND ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_06, SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua) = 7 AND ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_07, SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua) = 8 AND 
                         ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_08, SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua) = 9 AND ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_09, SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua) = 10 AND 
                         ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_10, SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua) = 11 AND ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_11, SUM(CASE WHEN MONTH(c.Ziua) = 12 AND 
                         ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_12, SUM(CASE WHEN ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CO_An, SUM(CASE WHEN ValStr = 'CM' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS CM_An, ISNULL(p.zile, 0) AS Solicitate, 
                         ISNULL(q.zile, 0) AS Planificate, ISNULL(b.SoldAnterior, 0) + ISNULL(b.Cuvenite, 0) - ISNULL(b.Efectuate, 0) - ISNULL(p.zile, 0) - ISNULL(q.zile, 0) - SUM(CASE WHEN ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) 
                         AS RamaseDePlanificat, ISNULL(b.SoldAnterior, 0) + ISNULL(b.Cuvenite, 0) - ISNULL(b.Efectuate, 0) - SUM(CASE WHEN ValStr = 'CO' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS RamaseDeEf, ISNULL(b.SoldAnterior, 0) 
                         + ISNULL(b.Cuvenite, 0) - ISNULL(b.Efectuate, 0) - SUM(CASE WHEN ValStr = 'CO' AND MONTH(c.Ziua) <= month(getdate()) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS RamaseSfLunaCurenta, SUM(CASE WHEN ValStr = 'CO' AND 
                         MONTH(c.Ziua) <= month(getdate()) THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS EfectuateLunaCurenta, u2.F70104 AS EID_manager, fm.F10003 AS marca_manager, fm.F10008 + ' ' + fm.F10009 AS nume_manager, 
                         u2.Mail AS mail_manager, a.F10078 AS angajator, ISNULL(b.Efectuate, 0) + SUM(CASE WHEN ValStr = 'CO' AND Ziua <= GETDATE() THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS Bis_Efect, ISNULL(w.zile, 0) 
                         + SUM(CASE WHEN ValStr = 'CO' AND Ziua > GETDATE() THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS Bis_Planif, ISNULL(b.SoldAnterior, 0) + ISNULL(b.Cuvenite, 0) - ISNULL(b.Efectuate, 0) - SUM(CASE WHEN ValStr = 'CO' AND 
                         Ziua <= GETDATE() THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS Bis_RamasEfec, ISNULL(b.SoldAnterior, 0) + ISNULL(b.Cuvenite, 0) - ISNULL(b.Efectuate, 0) - SUM(CASE WHEN ValStr = 'CO' AND Ziua <= GETDATE() 
                         THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) - ISNULL(w.zile, 0) - SUM(CASE WHEN ValStr = 'CO' AND Ziua > GETDATE() THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS Bis_RamasPlanif, ISNULL(z.cerere10zile, 0) AS cerere10zile
FROM            dbo.F100 AS fm LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.F004 ON dbo.F004.F00405 = fm.F10005 RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                             (SELECT        F10001, F10002, F10003, F10004, F10005, F10006, F10007, F10008, F10009, F100894, F10022, F10023, F10017, F10052, F10053, F10061, F10078
                               FROM            dbo.F100
                               WHERE        (F10025 = 0) AND (YEAR(F10023) >= @Anul)) AS a INNER JOIN
                         dbo.F005 AS f ON a.F10006 = f.F00506 INNER JOIN
                         dbo.F006 AS g ON a.F10007 = g.F00607 LEFT OUTER JOIN
                             (SELECT        F10003, Ziua, F06204, ZiSapt, ZiLibera, Parinte, Linia, Norma, F10002, F10004, F10005, F10006, F10007, ValStr, Val0, Val1, Val2, Val3, Val4, In1, Out1, In2, Out2, In3, Out3, In4, Out4, In5, Out5, In6, 
                                                         Out6, In7, Out7, In8, Out8, In9, Out9, In10, Out10, In11, Out11, In12, Out12, In13, Out13, In14, Out14, In15, Out15, In16, Out16, In17, Out17, In18, Out18, In19, Out19, In20, Out20, F1, F2, F3, F4, F5, 
                                                         F6, F7, F8, F9, F10, F11, F12, F13, F14, F15, F16, F17, F18, F19, F20, IdAuto, USER_NO, TIME, IdContract, IdProgram, FirstIn, LastOut, FirstInRap, LastOutRap, FirstInPaid, LastOutPaid, 
                                                         TimpLucratReal, TimpPauzaReal, CuloareValoare, F21, F22, F23, F24, F25, F26, F27, F28, F29, F30
                               FROM            dbo.Ptj_Intrari
                               WHERE        (YEAR(Ziua) = @Anul)) AS c ON a.F10003 = c.F10003 LEFT OUTER JOIN
                             (SELECT        F10003, An, Cuvenite, SoldAnterior, Efectuate, USER_NO, TIME, IdAuto
                               FROM            dbo.Ptj_tblZileCO
                               WHERE        (An = @Anul)) AS b ON a.F10003 = b.F10003 LEFT OUTER JOIN
                             (SELECT        F10003, SUM(ISNULL(NrZile, 0) - ISNULL(NrZileViitor, 0)) AS zile
                               FROM            dbo.Ptj_Cereri
                               WHERE        (IdStare IN (1, 2)) AND (YEAR(DataInceput) = @Anul) AND (IdAbsenta = 1)
                               GROUP BY F10003) AS p ON a.F10003 = p.F10003 LEFT OUTER JOIN
                             (SELECT        F10003, SUM(ISNULL(NrZile, 0) - ISNULL(NrZileViitor, 0)) AS zile
                               FROM            dbo.Ptj_Cereri AS Ptj_Cereri_1
                               WHERE        (IdStare = 4) AND (YEAR(DataInceput) = @Anul) AND (IdAbsenta = 1)
                               GROUP BY F10003) AS q ON a.F10003 = q.F10003 LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.USERS AS u1 ON a.F10003 = u1.F10003 LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.F062 ON a.F10053 = dbo.F062.F06204 LEFT OUTER JOIN
                             (SELECT        F10003, IdSuper, IdUser, USER_NO, TIME, IdAuto
                               FROM            dbo.F100Supervizori
                               WHERE        (IdSuper = 4)) AS sup ON a.F10003 = sup.F10003 LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.USERS AS u2 ON sup.IdUser = u2.F70102 ON fm.F10003 = u2.F10003 LEFT OUTER JOIN
                             (SELECT        F10003, SUM(ISNULL(NrZile, 0) - ISNULL(NrZileViitor, 0)) AS zile
                               FROM            dbo.Ptj_Cereri AS Ptj_Cereri_2
                               WHERE        (IdStare IN (1, 2, 4)) AND (YEAR(DataInceput) = @Anul) AND (IdAbsenta = 1)
                               GROUP BY F10003) AS w ON a.F10003 = w.F10003 LEFT OUTER JOIN
                             (SELECT        F10003, ISNULL(MAX(CASE WHEN DataSfarsit - DataInceput >= 10 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END), 0) AS cerere10zile
                               FROM            dbo.Ptj_Cereri AS Ptj_Cereri_3
                               WHERE        (IdAbsenta = 1) AND (IdStare IN (1, 2, 3))
                               GROUP BY F10003) AS z ON z.F10003 = a.F10003
GROUP BY a.F10003, a.F10017, a.F10052, a.F10008, a.F10009, a.F100894, f.F00507, g.F00608, a.F10022, a.F10023, b.Cuvenite, b.Efectuate, b.SoldAnterior, p.zile, q.zile, dbo.F062.F06205, u1.F70104, u2.F70104, u2.Mail, 
                         fm.F10008, fm.F10009, fm.F10003, a.F10078, dbo.F004.F00406, w.zile, z.cerere10zile, g.F00607, f.F00506, dbo.F004.F00405
) ZileCO_BIS
 
inner join F100 a on a.F10003 = ZileCO_BIS.Marca
left join F002 on a.F10002 = F002.F00202
left join F003 on a.F10004 = F003.F00304
 
left join F004 on a.F10005 = F004.F00405 
left join F005 on a.F10006 = F005.F00506
left join F006 on a.F10007=F006.F00607 
left outer join f062 on a.f10053 = f062.f06204

where  
(@UserId in (select distinct iduser from relgrupuser where idgrup in (0,4,6))) 
or 
(zileco_bis.marca in (select distinct f100supervizori.f10003 from f100supervizori where f100supervizori.idsuper in (1,2,4,5,6, 7) and @UserId = iduser)) 
or   
(zileco_bis.marca in (select distinct F10003 from users where f70102=@UserId))

 order by nume' with parameters:

                        SELECT A.F10003, 0 AS "Rol",  COALESCE((SELECT COALESCE("Alias", "Denumire") FROM "tblSupervizori" WHERE "Id"=0),'Angajat') AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        WHERE A.F10003 = -99
                        UNION
                        SELECT A.F10003, B."IdSuper" AS "Rol", CASE WHEN D."Alias" IS NOT NULL AND D."Alias" <> '' THEN D."Alias" ELSE D."Denumire" END AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" B ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        LEFT JOIN "tblSupervizori" D ON D."Id" = B."IdSuper"
                        WHERE B."IdUser"= 3) B                        
                        INNER JOIN F100 A ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        LEFT JOIN F718 X ON A.F10071=X.F71802
                        LEFT JOIN F003 F ON A.F10004 = F.F00304
                        LEFT JOIN F004 G ON A.F10005 = G.F00405
                        LEFT JOIN F005 H ON A.F10006 = H.F00506
                        LEFT JOIN F006 I ON A.F10007 = I.F00607

                        SELECT A.F10003, 0 AS "Rol",  COALESCE((SELECT COALESCE("Alias", "Denumire") FROM "tblSupervizori" WHERE "Id"=0),'Angajat') AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        WHERE A.F10003 = -99
                        UNION
                        SELECT A.F10003, B."IdSuper" AS "Rol", CASE WHEN D."Alias" IS NOT NULL AND D."Alias" <> '' THEN D."Alias" ELSE D."Denumire" END AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" B ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        LEFT JOIN "tblSupervizori" D ON D."Id" = B."IdSuper"
                        WHERE B."IdUser"= 3) B                        
                        INNER JOIN F100 A ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        LEFT JOIN F718 X ON A.F10071=X.F71802
                        LEFT JOIN F003 F ON A.F10004 = F.F00304
                        LEFT JOIN F004 G ON A.F10005 = G.F00405
                        LEFT JOIN F005 H ON A.F10006 = H.F00506
                        LEFT JOIN F006 I ON A.F10007 = I.F00607

Eroarea:   SELECT A.F10003, A.F10008 + ' ' + A.F10009 AS "NumeComplet", 
                        X.F71804 AS "Functia", F.F00305 AS "Subcompanie",G.F00406 AS "Filiala",H.F00507 AS "Sectie",I.F00608 AS "Departament" , "Rol", "RolDenumire"
                        FROM (
                        SELECT A.F10003, 0 AS "Rol",  COALESCE((SELECT COALESCE("Alias", "Denumire") FROM "tblSupervizori" WHERE "Id"=0),'Angajat') AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        WHERE A.F10003 = -99
                        UNION
                        SELECT A.F10003, B."IdSuper" AS "Rol", CASE WHEN D."Alias" IS NOT NULL AND D."Alias" <> '' THEN D."Alias" ELSE D."Denumire" END AS "RolDenumire"
                        FROM F100 A
                        INNER JOIN "F100Supervizori" B ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        LEFT JOIN "tblSupervizori" D ON D."Id" = B."IdSuper"
                        WHERE B."IdUser"= 3) B                        
                        INNER JOIN F100 A ON A.F10003=B.F10003
                        LEFT JOIN F718 X ON A.F10071=X.F71802
                        LEFT JOIN F003 F ON A.F10004 = F.F00304
                        LEFT JOIN F004 G ON A.F10005 = G.F00405
